     <header role="presentation" class="m-heading-2"> 
      <h2 class="c-heading-3">Frequently asked questions</h2> 
     </header> 
    </div> 
   </div> 
   <div id="bottomregion" data-grid="container" data-region-key="bottomregion" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;bottomregion 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Region_coreui-region&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:12,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;a2&quot;}"> 
    <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;faqs 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r12a2&quot;}" data-module-id="Office.ProductTemplate|bottomregion|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
     <section class="cui-drawer"> 
      <div class="cui-header "> 
       <div class="cui-drawer-toggle"> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Expand all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m1r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m1r12a2&quot;}" class="f-expand c-action-toggle" name="Expand all" data-toggled-label="Expand all" aria-label="Expand all questions and answers">Expand all</button> <span>|</span> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Collapse all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m1r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m1r12a2&quot;}" class="f-collapse c-action-toggle" name="Collapse all" data-toggled-label="Collapse all" aria-label="Collapse all questions and answers" disabled>Collapse all</button> 
       </div> 
       <div style="clear: both;"></div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m1r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m1r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1-collapsible-drawer0">Who is your frontline workforce?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Frontline workers and managers are shift-based, mobile-first workers. They have various names, such as frontline workers and essential workers, but at their core theyre the people first to have contact with your customers, first to work with your product, and first to represent your brand. They are your store associates, customer service representatives, nurses, doctors, factory operators, and more.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m1r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m1r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1-collapsible-drawer1">In what products are the frontline worker capabilities available?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>The frontline worker capabilities are available in all commercial offerings. Some of these capabilities are not available in the free version of Teams or Government offerings.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m1r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m1r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1-collapsible-drawer2">Where can I learn more about ways to use Teams for my frontline workforce?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Learn more about empowering your frontline workforce with Teams&nbsp;<a aria-label="Read the blog about empowering frontline workers" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2115428">here</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m1r12a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m1r12a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1-collapsible-drawer3">What happened to StaffHub?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-95md5z1-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Effective June 30, 2020, Microsoft StaffHub was retired. StaffHub capabilities are being built into Teams. <a aria-label="Learn more about StaffHub capabilities being built into Teams" class="c-hyperlink" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2093391">Learn more</a></p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div>
